// The Monsters
Actor PsxZombieman_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterHumanoidMedium replaces Zombieman2
{
	Health 20
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Speed 8
	PainChance 200
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
	SeeSound "grunt/sight"
	AttackSound "grunt/attack"
	PainSound "grunt/pain"
	DeathSound "grunt/death"
	ActiveSound "grunt/active"
	Obituary "$OB_ZOMBIE"
	DropItem "Clip2"
	Tag "Zombieman"
	Species "SamsaraZombieman"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		POSS AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		POSS AABBCCDD 4 A_Chase
		Loop
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		POSS E 10 A_FaceTarget
		POSS F 8 A_CustomBulletAttack(22.5, 0, 1, random(1,5) * 3, "BulletPuff", 0, CBAF_NORANDOM)
		POSS E 8
		Goto See
	Pain:
		POSS G 2
		POSS G 4 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Pain.DoomDamageTypeStunner:
		POSS G 2 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",true)
		POSS G 300 A_Pain
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",false)
		Goto See
	Pain.MightyBoot:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/kickhit",CHAN_BODY)
		POSS G 2 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
		POSS G 16 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		POSS H 4 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		POSS I 6 A_Scream
		POSS J 4 A_NoBlocking
		POSS K 6
		POSS L -1
		Stop
	Death.CalebFire:
	Death.LifeLeech:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(218, 2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("CalebDMTaunt1", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodBurningCorpse_Generic", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 5 A_NoBlocking
		Stop
	Death.PainkillerStake:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	StakeDeath:
		POSS H 2
		Loop
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		POSS M 4 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		POSS N 6 A_XScream
		POSS O 4 A_NoBlocking
		POSS P 6
		POSS Q 4
		POSS R 6
		POSS S 4
		POSS T 6
		POSS U -1
		Stop
	Raise:
		POSS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyZorched",1,"ZorchRaise")
		POSS K 5
		POSS JIH 5
		Goto See
	ZorchRaise:
		"####" "#" 1 A_UnsetShootable
		"####" "#" 1 A_SpawnItem("SpawnFire2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("archvile/resummon")
		"####" "#" 1 A_TakeInventory("EnemyZorched",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.2,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.3,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.4,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.5,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetShootable
		Goto See
	Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		POSS G 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxZombieman_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxZombieman_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxZombieman_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxZombieman_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxZombieman_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxZombieman_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxZombieman_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxZombieman_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		POSS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		POSS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}
}

actor PsxZombieman_Samsara_Shrink : PsxZombieman_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 8
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			POSS G 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			POSS AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			POSS A 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			POSS A 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			POSS B 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			POSS B 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			POSS C 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			POSS C 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			POSS D 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			POSS D 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxZombieman_Samsara", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			Stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			Loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			Stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}

actor PsxZombieman_Samsara_ShrinkEffect : PsxZombieman_Samsara
{
	-ISMONSTER
	-COUNTKILL
	-SHOOTABLE
	-SOLID
	+NOINTERACTION
	-NOGRAVITY
	Renderstyle Translucent
	Alpha 0.4
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			POSS G 0
			POSS G 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			POSS G 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			CPOS C 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CPOS D 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CPOS D 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxChaingunguy_Samsara", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			Stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			Loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			Stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

Actor PsxDoomImp_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterHumanoidMedium replaces DoomImp2
{
	Health 60
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 100
	Speed 8
	PainChance 200
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
	+NOTDMATCH
	+NOICEDEATH
	SeeSound "imp/sight"
	PainSound "imp/pain"
	DeathSound "imp/death"
	ActiveSound "imp/active"
	HitObituary "$OB_IMPHIT"
	Obituary "$OB_IMP"
	Tag "Imp"
	Species "SamsaraDoomImp"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TROO AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		TROO A 2 A_Chase
		TROO A 4 A_Chase
		TROO B 2 A_Chase
		TROO B 4 A_Chase
		TROO C 2 A_Chase
		TROO C 4 A_Chase
		TROO D 2 A_Chase
		TROO D 4 A_Chase
		Loop
	Melee:
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		TROO EF 8 A_FaceTarget
		TROO G 6 A_CustomComboAttack("PsxDoomImpBall2", 32, 3 * random(1, 8), "imp/melee")
		Goto See
	Pain:
		TROO H 2
		TROO H 2 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Pain.DoomDamageTypeStunner:
		TROO H 2 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",true)
		TROO H 300 A_Pain
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",false)
		Goto See
	Pain.MightyBoot:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/kickhit",CHAN_BODY)
		TROO H 2 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
		TROO H 16 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TROO I 8 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TROO J 8 A_Scream
		TROO K 6
		TROO L 6 A_NoBlocking
		TROO M -1
		Stop
	Death.CalebFire:
	Death.LifeLeech:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(218, 2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("CalebDMTaunt1", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodBurningCorpse_Generic", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 5 A_NoBlocking
		Stop
	Death.PainkillerStake:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	StakeDeath:
		TROO H 2
		Loop
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TROO N 4 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TROO O 6 A_XScream
		TROO P 4
		TROO Q 6 A_NoBlocking
		TROO R 4
		TROO S 6
		TROO T 4
		TROO U -1
		Stop
	Raise:
		TROO A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyZorched",1,"ZorchRaise")
		TROO ML 8
		TROO KJI 6
		Goto See
	ZorchRaise:
		"####" "#" 1 A_UnsetShootable
		"####" "#" 1 A_SpawnItem("SpawnFire2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("archvile/resummon")
		"####" "#" 1 A_TakeInventory("EnemyZorched",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.2,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.3,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.4,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.5,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetShootable
		Goto See
	Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		TROO G 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxDoomImp_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxDoomImp_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxDoomImp_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxDoomImp_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxDoomImp_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxDoomImp_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxDoomImp_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxDoomImp_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		TROO A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		TROO A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}

actor PsxDoomImp_Samsara_Shrink : PsxDoomImp_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 8
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			TROO G 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			TROO AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			TROO A 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			TROO A 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			TROO A 4 A_Chase("","")

Actor PsxDemon_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterDemonicMediumTotalGib replaces DoomDemon2
{
	Health 150
	PainChance 180
	Speed 10
	Radius 30
	Height 56
	Mass 400
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
	+NOTDMATCH
	+NOICEDEATH
	SeeSound "demon/sight"
	AttackSound "demon/melee"
	PainSound "demon/pain"
	DeathSound "demon/death"
	ActiveSound "demon/active"
	Obituary "$OB_DEMONHIT"
	Tag "Demon"
	Species "SamsaraDemon"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		SARG AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		SARG AABBCCDD 2 Fast A_Chase
		Loop
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		SARG EF 8 Fast A_FaceTarget
		SARG G 8 A_SargAttack
		Goto See
	Pain:
		SARG H 2 Fast
		SARG H 2 Fast A_Pain
		Goto See
	Pain.DoomDamageTypeStunner:
		SARG H 2 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",true)
		SARG H 300 A_Pain
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",false)
		Goto See
	Pain.MightyBoot:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/kickhit",CHAN_BODY)

		TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(12)
		SARG H 16 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		SARG I 8 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		SARG J 8 A_Scream
		SARG K 4
		SARG L 4 A_NoBlocking
		SARG M 4
		SARG N -1
		Stop
	Death.ZorchPistol:
	Death.Zorch:
	Death.ZorchKamikaze:
	Death.PhasingZorch:

	Death.PainkillerStake:

		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking

		Loop
	Raise:
		SARG A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyZorched",1,"ZorchRaise")

		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.5,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)

		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetShootable
		Goto See
	Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		SARG G 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)

		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)

		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		SARG A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}
}

actor PsxDemon_Samsara_Shrink : PsxDemon_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 8
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			SARG H 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			SARG AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG A 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			SARG A 2 A_Chase("","")

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG B 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG C 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG C 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			SARG D 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			SARG D 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			Stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			Loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)

			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			Stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

		TNT1 A 2

		SARG A 0

		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)

		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)

		SARG A 0

			SARG H 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			SARG AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")

			SARG A 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly

			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			Stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			Loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)

			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			Stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

Actor PsxLostSoul_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterSkeletonSmall replaces LostSoul2
{
	Health 60
	Radius 16
	Height 56
	Mass 50
	Speed 8
	Damage 3
	PainChance 256
	Monster
	+FLOAT
	+NOGRAVITY
	+MISSILEMORE
	+DONTFALL
	+NOICEDEATH
	+NOBLOOD
	+NOTDMATCH
	+RETARGETAFTERSLAM
	AttackSound "skull/melee"
	PainSound "skull/pain"
	DeathSound "skull/death"
	ActiveSound "skull/active"
	Obituary "$OB_SKULL"
	Tag "Lost Soul"
	Species "SamsaraLostSoul"
	RenderStyle "Normal" // gzdoom
	DamageFactor "LostSoul64Explosion", 0
	+NOBLOOD
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		SKUL A 0 bright NoDelay A_GiveInventory("IsAFlyingActor")
	Spawn2:
		SKUL AB 10 bright A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		SKUL AB 6 bright A_Chase
		Loop
	Missile:
		SKUL C 10 bright A_FaceTarget
		SKUL D 4 bright A_SkullAttack
		SKUL CD 4 bright
		Goto Missile+2
	Pain:
		SKUL E 2 bright
		SKUL E 4 bright A_Pain
		Goto See
	Pain.DoomDamageTypeStunner:
		SKUL E 2 bright A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",true)
		SKUL E 300 bright A_Pain
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",false)
		Goto See
	Pain.MightyBoot:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/kickhit",CHAN_BODY)
		SKUL E 2 bright A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
		SKUL E 16 bright A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		SKUL F 6 bright ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		SKUL G 6 bright A_Scream
		SKUL H 6 bright
		SKUL I 6 bright A_NoBlocking
		SKUL JK 6
		Stop
	}
}

Actor PsxPainElemental_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterReincPainElemental replaces PainElemental2
{
	Health 400
	Radius 31
	Height 56
	Mass 400
	Speed 8
	PainChance 128
	Monster
	+FLOAT
	+NOGRAVITY
	+NOTDMATCH
	+NOICEDEATH
	SeeSound "pain/sight"
	PainSound "pain/pain"
	DeathSound "pain/death"
	ActiveSound "pain/active"
	Tag "Pain Elemental"
	Species "SamsaraPainElemental"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		PAIN A 0 NoDelay A_GiveInventory("IsAFlyingActor")
	Spawn2:
		PAIN A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		PAIN AABBCC 4 A_Chase
		Loop

		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)

		PAIN G 6 A_Pain
		Goto See

		Goto See
	Pain.MightyBoot:

		PAIN L 8 bright A_PainDie("PsxLostSoul_Samsara")
		PAIN M 8 bright
		Stop
	Raise:
		PAIN MLKJIH 8
		Goto See
	Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		PAIN G 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxPainElemental_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxPainElemental_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxPainElemental_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxPainElemental_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxPainElemental_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxPainElemental_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxPainElemental_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxPainElemental_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		PAIN A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")

		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)

		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)

		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		PAIN A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	SpawnTheLostSoul:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PainDie("PsxLostSoul_Samsara")
		Stop
	SpawnTheLostSoulPK:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PainDie("PsxLostSoul_Samsara")
		TNT1 A 350 // Needed for souls to appear when gibbed
		Wait
	}

	Speed 1

			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			PAIN G 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			PAIN A 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)

actor PsxCacodemon_Samsara_Shrink : PsxCacodemon_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 8
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			HEAD E 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			HEAD A 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			HEAD A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxCacodemon_Samsara", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			Stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			Loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			Stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxBaronOfHell_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxBaronOfHell_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxBaronOfHell_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxBaronOfHell_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxBaronOfHell_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("VULNERABLE", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("SHOOTABLE", 0)
		Goto ShrunkLoop
	ShrunkLoop:
		TNT1 A 2 A_JumpIfInventory("MasterDeadToken",1,"ShrunkDie")
		Loop
	ShrunkDie:
		TNT1 A 1 A_Die("Shrink")
		Stop
	Death.Shrink:
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraBossDeathToggler")
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		BOSS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetDamageType("DukeExplosive")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode((height * 2) * 1.75, 80)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraBossDeathToggler")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		BOSS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraBossDeathToggler")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}

actor PsxBaronOfHell_Samsara_Shrink : PsxBaronOfHell_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	-COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			BOSS H 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			BOSS AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:

		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetShootable
		Goto See
	Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		BOS2 H 0

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxHellKnight_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxHellKnight_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("VULNERABLE", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("SHOOTABLE", 0)
		Goto ShrunkLoop
	ShrunkLoop:
		TNT1 A 2 A_JumpIfInventory("MasterDeadToken",1,"ShrunkDie")
		Loop
	ShrunkDie:
		TNT1 A 1 A_Die("Shrink")
		Stop

		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraBossDeathToggler")
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		BOS2 A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetDamageType("DukeExplosive")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Explode((height * 2) * 1.75, 80)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraBossDeathToggler")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		BOS2 A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraBossDeathToggler")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}

{

	+VULNERABLE

	MaxDropOffHeight 0

	Height 16

	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			BOS2 H 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			BOS2 AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)

			BOS2 A 3 A_Chase("","")

			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			Stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)

			Loop

			TNT1 A 0
			Stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")

		Stop

	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		FATT A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraBossDeathToggler")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}

		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraBossDeathToggler")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}
}

	{

		Loop

		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)

		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxArchvile_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxArchvile_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)

		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PsxArchvile_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		VILE A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		VILE A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		Loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}

Actor PsxWolfensteinSS_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterHumanoidMedium replaces PsxWolfensteinSS
{
	Health 50
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Speed 8
	PainChance 170
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
	+THRUGHOST
	+NOTDMATCH
	+NOICEDEATH
	SeeSound "wolfss/sight"
	PainSound "wolfss/pain"
	DeathSound "wolfss/death"
	ActiveSound "wolfss/active"
	AttackSound "wolfss/attack"
	Obituary "$OB_WOLFSS"
	DropItem "Clip2"
	Tag "Nazi"
	Species "SamsaraWolfensteinSS"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		SSWV AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		SSWV AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
		Loop
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		SSWV EF 10 A_FaceTarget
		SSWV G 4 bright A_CustomBulletAttack(22.5, 0, 1, random(1,5) * 3, "BulletPuff", 0, CBAF_NORANDOM)
		SSWV F 6 A_FaceTarget
		SSWV G 4 bright A_CustomBulletAttack(22.5, 0, 1, random(1,5) * 3, "BulletPuff", 0, CBAF_NORANDOM)
		SSWV F 1 A_CPosRefire
		Goto Missile+2
	Pain:
		SSWV H 3
		SSWV H 3 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Pain.DoomDamageTypeStunner:
		SSWV H 2 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",true)
		SSWV H 300 A_Pain
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",false)
		Goto See
	Pain.MightyBoot:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/kickhit",CHAN_BODY)
		SSWV H 2 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
		SSWV H 16 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		SSWV I 5 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)

		SSWV K 5 A_NoBlocking

		SSWV M -1

	Death.CalebFire:

		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 5 A_NoBlocking
		Stop
	Death.PainkillerStake:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	StakeDeath:
		SSWV H 2
		Loop
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		SSWV N 5 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		SSWV O 5 A_XScream
		SSWV P 5 A_NoBlocking
		SSWV QRSTU 5
		SSWV V -1
		Stop
	Raise:
		SSWV A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyZorched",1,"ZorchRaise")
		SSWV MLKJI 5
		Goto See
	ZorchRaise:
		"####" "#" 1 A_UnsetShootable
		"####" "#" 1 A_SpawnItem("SpawnFire2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("archvile/resummon")
		"####" "#" 1 A_TakeInventory("EnemyZorched",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.2,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.3,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.4,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.5,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetShootable
		Goto See
	Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		SSWV H 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
